        });

        lazyLoadElements.forEach(element => {
            observer.observe(element);
        });
    } else {
        // Fallback for browsers without IntersectionObserver support
        lazyLoadElements.forEach(placeholder => {
            let contentId = placeholder.dataset.content;
            let file_list_html = '';
            switch(contentId) {
